2003-01-17 09:50:59 Running '/bin/cat /etc/profile'
                    #ident      "@(#)profile    1.14    93/08/24 SMI"   /* SVr4.0 1.3   */
                    if [ $HOME = "/" ]
                    then
                        if [[ $LOGNAME != "root" ]]
                        then
                                exit
                        fi
                    fi

                    # The profile that all logins get before using their own .profile.

                    stty erase
                    stty intr

                    trap "" 2 3
                    export EPAGE_HOME=/opt/DMC/epage
                    OPENWINHOME=/usr/openwin
                    INFORMIXDIR=/usr/informix
                    PATH=$PATH:.:/var/SUNWspro/bin:/usr/ccs/bin:/var/SUNWxt/bin:$INFORMIXDIR/bin:$OPENWINHOME/bin:/etc:/usr/local/bin:/usr/ccs/bin:/db/tools/bin:/usr/ucb:/usr/lib/hpnp/bin:/mnt/dt/bin:/opt/DMC/epage/bin:/opt/UWpine/bin:/usr/sbin:/usr/ar/bin
                    MANPATH=/var/SUNWspro/man:/usr/man:$MANPATH:/usr/lib/hpnp/man
                    TZ=MST7MDT
                    EDITOR=vi
                    OPENWINHOME=/usr/openwin
                    APOP=\"/etc/pop.auth\"
                    POPUID=\"pop\"
                    MACHNAME=`uname -n`
                    PSORT_NPROCS=4
                    PSORT_DBTEMP=/tmp
                    LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/usr/lib:/var/SUNWspro/lib:$OPENWINHOME/lib:/usr/lib/hpnp/lib
                    export LOGNAME INFORMIXDIR PATH TZ EDITOR OPENWINHOME MACHNAME PSORT_NPROCS
                    export PSORT_DBTEMP MANPATH LD_LIBRARY_PATH
                    #PS1="romulus# "
                    #PS1="$MACHNAME:$LOGNAME:<$(tildize $PWD)># "
                    # See below for definition of PS1 -- it must reside below the "tildize" function
                    PS2=">> "

                      sccscreate() { date "+%D %T";/usr/local/scripts/sccscreate.sh "$@" ; }
                      sccsdelget() { date "+%D %T";/usr/local/scripts/sccsdelget.sh "$@" ; }
                      sccsedit  () { date "+%D %T";/usr/local/scripts/sccsedit.sh   "$@" ; }
                      sccsget   () { date "+%D %T";/usr/local/scripts/sccsget.sh    "$@" ; }
                      sccsrmdel () { date "+%D %T";/usr/local/scripts/sccsrmdel.sh  "$@" ; }
                      sccsunedit() { date "+%D %T";/usr/local/scripts/sccsunedit.sh "$@" ; }

                    if [ "$TERM" = "" ]
                    then
                        TERM=wyse60
                        export TERM
                    fi

                    #   Login and -su shells get /etc/profile services.
                    #   -rsh is given its environment in its .profile.

                    case "$0" in
                    -sh | -ksh | -jsh )

                        if [ ! -f .hushlogin ]
                        then
                                /usr/sbin/quota
                                #       Allow the user to break the Message-Of-The-Day only.
                                trap "trap '' 2"  2
                                /bin/cat -s /etc/motd
                                trap "" 2

                                /bin/mail -E
                                case $? in
                                0)
                                        echo "You have new mail."
                                        ;;
                                2)
                                        echo "You have mail."
                                        ;;
                                esac
                        fi
                    esac

                    umask 022
                    trap  1 2 3 14 15
                    ##trap "exit" 15

                    tildize() {
                       if [[ $1 != "/home"* ]]; then
                          print "$1"
                          return 0
                       fi
                       if [[ $HOME != / && $1 = $HOME* ]]; then
                          print "\~${1#$HOME}"
                          return 0
                       fi
                       awk '{FS=":"; print $1, $6}' /etc/passwd |
                          while read user homedir; do
                             if [[ $homedir != / && $1 = ${homedir}?(/*) ]]; then
                                print "\~$user${1#$homedir}"
                                return 0
                             fi
                          done
                       print "$1"
                       return 1
                    }

                    _cd() {
                       "cd" "$@"
                       es=$?
                       PS1="`hostname`:$LOGNAME:<($PWD)># "
                       return $es
                    }

                    PS1="$MACHNAME:$LOGNAME:<($PWD)># "
                    alias cd=_cd
                    export PS1 PS2

                    wyse60() {
                       TERM=wyse60 export TERM
                    }

                    title() {
                       /usr/5bin/echo -n "\033]l$*\033\"
                       /usr/5bin/echo -n "\033]L$*\033\"
                    }

                    l() {
                       ls -l
                    }

                    la() {
                       ls -lia
                    }

                    lm() {
                       ls -l | more
                    }

                    ldir() {
                       ls -altr | grep "^d"
                    }

                    lg() {
                       ls -lg
                    }

                    l4() {
                       ls -l *.4gl
                    }

                    lper() {
                       ls -l *.per
                    }

                    l4i() {
                       ls -l *.4gi
                    }
                    LPHOME=/usr/lpplus;export LPHOME
                    PATH="$PATH:${LPHOME}/bin";export PATH
